| 1.  आवेिक का नाि (बडे अक्षरों ि)ें                    |                 |                   |                       |                |     |
| 2.  जपन कोड, आजधकाररक टेलीफोन नंबर और िोबाइल नंबर और  |                 |                   |                       |                |     |

44 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
आजधकाररक ई-िेल आईडी के साथ पूरा पता
3. आवेिक की जस्ट्थजत िाव ेराज्य सरकार वो या केंर िाजसत प्रििे या
जवश्वजवयालालय या रस्ट्ट
4. पंिीकरण या जनगिन (संख्या और किनांक, यकि कोई वो)
5. सोवा-ररग्पा िवाजवयालालयका नाि और पता
6. राज्य सरकार या केंर िाजसत प्रिेि प्रिासन द्वारा िारी 'अनापजत्त प्रिाण
पत्र' या 'अजनवायषता प्रिाण पत्र' की जतजथ
7. िालू िैक्षजणक वष ष के जलए कॉलेि या संस्ट्थान की अनुिजत की जस्ट्थजत
8. i. संबद्ध जवश्वजवयालालय का नाि और पता
ii. प्रथि संबद्धता की जतजथ
iii. पररयोिना के जलए प्रथि सबं द्धता की जतजथ
9. स्नातक या स्नातकोत्तर पाठ्यक्रि िें प्रथि बैि के जलए प्रवेि का वषष
10. प्रथि प्रवेजित स्नातक या स्नातकोत्तर बैि के परू ा वोने का िवीना और वषष
11. िौिूिा स्नातक या स्नातकोत्तर पाठ्यक्रि के जलए आयुष िंत्रालय या
तत्कालीन भारतीय जिककत्सा प्रणाली के केंरीय पररषि या भारतीय
जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष द्वारा स्ट्वीकृत सीटों की संख्या
और िान्द्यता की तारीख
12. अध्ययन के प्रस्ट्ताजवत नए या उच्चतर पाठ्यक्रि का नाि
13. छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता या प्रवेि क्षिता (पंरव या सोलव से तीस तक) िें वृजद्ध
के जलए आवेिन की गई सीटों की संख्या जनर्िष्टष करें
14. जववरण
(ए) अजतररि जवत्तीय आवंटन -
(बी) अजतररि स्ट्थान, उपकरण और अन्द्य िलू भूत सुजवधाओं के जलए
प्रावधान -
(सी) छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता ि ेंवृजद्ध के संबंध ि ेंअजतररि स्ट्टाफ (जिक्षण
स्ट्टाफ, गैर-जिक्षण स्ट्टाफ और अस्ट्पताल स्ट्टाफ) की भती
15. अन्द्य प्रासंजगक िानकारी
स्ट्थान : __________________ आविे क के वस्ट्ताक्षर
परू ा नाि
किनाकं : __________________ पि
अनलु ग्नको की सिू ी:
1. सम्बंजधत राज्य सरकार या केंर िाजसत प्रििे प्रिासन द्वारा िारी 'अनापजत्त प्रिाणपत्र' की सत्याजपत प्रजत।
2. ककसी िान्द्यता प्राप्त जवश्वजवयालालय द्वारा िारी संबद्धता सविजत पत्र की सत्याजपत प्रजत।
3. िेजडकल कॉलेि या संस्ट्थान के जवत्तीय रैक ररकॉडष के बारे िें स्ट्वतंत्र पछू ताछ करने के जलए भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत
आकलन और रेटटंग बोडषया भारतीय जिककत्सा प्रणाली के जलए राष्ट्रीय आयोग को अजधकृत करने वाल ेआवेिक के बैंकरों को
संबोजधत प्राजधकरण पत्र।
4. आयुष िंत्रालय या पूवषवती केंरीय भारतीय जिककत्सा पररषि या भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडषस े
कॉलेि या संस्ट्थान की िान्द्यता को िंिूरी िेने वाले पत्र की सत्याजपत प्रजत, यकि पवल े से वी स्नातक जडग्री कायषक्रि
आयोजित करने की अनुिजत व।ै
5. वलफनाि े िें कवा गया व ै कक छात्रों को "सोवा-ररग्पा स्नातक के जलए राष्ट्रीय भारतीय जिककत्सा प्रणाली-राष्ट्रीय पात्रता-
सव-प्रवेि परीक्षा" योग्यता के आधार पर और केवल सोवा-ररग्पा केंरीय परािि ष के िाध्यि से और भारतीय जिककत्सा
पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडद्वष ारा जनर्िष्टष स्ट्वीकृत छात्र प्रविे क्षिता से परे प्रवेि किया िाएगा।
6 िपथ पत्र िें यव जलखा वोना िाजवए कक संबंजधत जवजनयिों िें उजल्लजखत छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता के संबंध िें छात्र-जिक्षक
अनुपात के अनुसार िानव संसाधन बनाए रखा िाएगा।

7. आवेिन िुल्क और ििा की गई प्रोसेलसंग फीस का प्रिाण।
8. अन्द्य अनलु ग्नकों
ए. रजस्ट्टयों के नाि के साथ उपजनयि या ज्ञापन और एसोजसएिन के लेख या रस्ट्ट डीड की प्रिाजणत प्रजत और
रस्ट्ट या सोसायटी पंिीकरण या जनगिन की नवीनीकृत प्रजत।
बी. स्ट्वाजित्व या पट्टा सिझौते के प्रिाण के रूप िें भूजि िस्ट्तावेिों की प्रिाजणत प्रजत।
सी. िौिूिा अस्ट्पताल के स्ट्वाजित्व के प्रिाण के रूप िें पवला अस्ट्पताल पंिीकरण प्रिाणपत्र या नवीनीकृत।
डी. अजग्न सुरक्षा प्रिाणपत्र।
ई. आपिा प्रबंधन प्रिाणपत्र (यकि कोई वो) ।
एफ. प्रिषू ण जनयंत्रण प्रिाण पत्र।
िी. बायोिेजडकल अपजिष्ट प्रबधं न सिझौता।
एि. कॉलेि और अस्ट्पताल भवन अजधभोग प्रिाण पत्र।
| आई. कॉलेि एवं अस्ट्पताल भवन पणू | षता प्रिाण पत्र।  |     |     |     |
| ------------------------------- | ----------------- | --- | --- | --- |
ि.े  जबलल्डंग प्लान स्ट्थानीय प्राजधकारी द्वारा अनुिोकित और वास्ट्तुकार द्वारा सिर्थषत।
के. इन जवजनयिों के अनुसार वास्ट्तुकार द्वारा अजधकृत क्षेत्र जववरण प्रिाणपत्र।
एल. िौिूिा स्नातक कायषक्रि ि ेंप्रवेि क्षिता बढाने के जलए उपकरण, उपकरण आकि के जबल खरीिें।
| एि. जपछल ेएक वष ष | के जबलों के साथ तैयार या खरीिी गई िवाओं की सूिी।  |     |     |     |
| ----------------- | ------------------------------------------------- | --- | --- | --- |
एन. जपछले एक वषष के जबलों सजवत खरीिी गई कच्ची औषजधयों की सूिी।
ओ. अस्ट्पताल का सिेककत डेटा: जपछल े एक वषष के जलए रोगी डेटा (बाह्य रोगी जवभाग, आंतररक रोगी जवभाग
और जबस्ट्तर अजधभोग) ।
पी. अस्ट्पताल भवन सजवत भूजि, भवन के जलए भुगतान की गई कर रसीि।
क्य.ू  यव कवते हुए एक विन पत्र प्रस्ट्तुत करें कक संस्ट्थान भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग जनजध के पक्ष ि ें
| पांि साल की अवजध के जलए वधै |  जनजित सुरक्षा ििा राजि ििा करने ि ेंसक्षि व।ै |     |     |     |

9.  नए सोवा-ररग्पा िेजडकल कॉलिे  की स्ट्थापना के प्रस्ट्ताजवत क्षत्रे   ख़राब या पयाषप्त
िें नैिाजनक सािग्री (रोजगयों) की उपलब्लधता का िायरा

| 11.  राज्य सरकार द्वारा उन छात्रों पर, िो राज्य के जनवासी नवीं व,ैं |                                    |     |     |     |
| राज्य िें प्रवेि प्राप्त करन े                                      | पर लगाए गए प्रजतबंध, यकि कोई वों,  |     |     |     |
को जनर्िष्टष  करना वोगा
| 12.  प्रस्ट्ताजवत सोवा-ररग्पा िेजडकल कॉलेि खोलने का पूण ष |     |     | औजित्य  |     |
| --------------------------------------------------------- | --- | --- | ------- | --- |
अजनवायतष ा प्रिाणपत्र या अनापजत्त प्रिाणपत्र
अजनवायषता प्रिाण पत्र या अनापजत्त प्रिाण पत्र ---------------------------------- को िारी ककया िाता व ै ------------
(आवेिक का नाि) की स्ट्थापना के जलए ----------------------------------(प्रस्ट्ताजवत कॉलेि या संस्ट्थान का नाि) -----------
--------------------------(प्रस्ट्ताजवत कॉलेि या संस्ट्थान का पता) -------(पंरव या तीस) की छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता के साथ। यव
प्रिाणपत्र उपरोि जववरण, तथ्यों या ितों को ध्यान ि ेंरखते हुए िारी ककया िाता व।ै

यव प्रिाणपत्र प्रिाणपत्र िारी वोने की तारीख स ेलगातार िो िैक्षजणक सत्रों के जलए वैध व।ै

अजनवायतष ा प्रिाणपत्र या अनापजत्त प्रिाणपत्र जनम्नजलजखत जनयि और ितों पर िारी ककया िाता व:ै
1. कॉलेि भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग के तवत भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष से उजित
अनुिजत प्राप्त करने के बाि वी भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष द्वारा स्ट्वीकृत छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता के
अनुसार छात्रों को प्रवेि िेगा।
2. कॉलेि उसी पररसर िें कोई अन्द्य कॉलेि, पाठ्यक्रि या कायषक्रि आयोजित नवीं करेगा िब तक कक भारतीय जिककत्सा
पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोड षद्वारा अन्द्यथा अनुिजत न िी िाए।
3. कॉलेि छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता के अनुसार भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा जनर्िष्टष  बुजनयािी ढांि,े  िानव
संसाधन और कायषक्षिता के संिभष िें सभी न्द्यूनति आवश्यक िानकों को बनाए रखगे ा।
4. कॉलेि भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा अजधसूजित िौिूिा जनयिों, कििाजनिेिों और नीजतयों के अनुसार
" भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग-राष्ट्रीय पात्रता-सव-प्रवेि परीक्षा सोवा-ररग्पा स्नातक" पात्र छात्रों को प्रवेि
िेगा।
5. संस्ट्थान वर सिय स्ट्वायत्त बोडष, भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग, भारत सरकार और जवश्वजवयालालय द्वारा
जनधाषररत ितों का पालन करेगा।

| III—खण् ड 4] |     | भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण  |     |     |     |     |
| ------------ | --- | -------------------------- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [भाग         |     |                            |     |     |     | 47  |
6. कॉलेि को अन्द्य सोसायटी या रस्ट्ट को वस्ट्तांतररत करने की जस्ट्थजत िें, राज्य सरकार या केंर िाजसत प्रिेि प्रिासन,
िैसा भी िािला वो, से पूवष अनापजत्त प्रिाण पत्र प्राप्त ककया िाएगा।
7. यकि आवेिक भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोगद्वारा जनर्िष्टष  न्द्यूनति आवश्यक िानकों के अनुसार सोवा-ररग्पा
िेजडकल कॉलेि के जलए बुजनयािी ढांिे, िानव संसाधन और अन्द्य सुजवधाओं को बनान े या बनाए रखने ि ें जवफल रवता व,ै
तो िेजडकल द्वारा नए प्रवेि रोक किए िाते व।ैं  भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष और भारतीय जिककत्सा
पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोड;ष
या भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग की अनुिजत से जवश्वजवयालालय कॉलेि ि ें पवले स े वी प्रवेजित छात्रों की
जिम्िेिारी लेगा।
8. आयोग द्वारा जनधाषररत न्द्यूनति आवश्यक िानकों के जलए कॉलेि द्वारा अनुपालन न करन े के कारण भारतीय जिककत्सा
पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष द्वारा कॉलेि को अनुिजत िेन े से इनकार करन े या स्ट्थायी अस्ट्वीकृजत िारी करन े की जस्ट्थजत
ि,ें  राज्य सरकार कॉलेि को अपने अजधकार िें ले लेगी। उन छात्रों की जिम्िेिारी, जिन्द्व ें िेजडकल असेसिेंट एंड रेटटंग बोड ष
फॉर इंजडयन जसस्ट्टि ऑफ िेजडजसन की अनुिजत से पवले वी कॉलेि िें प्रवेि जिल िुका व।ै
(सक्षि प्राजधकारी के वस्ट्ताक्षर)

ि ेंिौििू ा स्नातक कायक्रष ि ि ेंसीटें या छात्र प्रविे  क्षिता या प्रविे  क्षिता बढान ेके जलए

48 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
अजनवायतष ा प्रिाणपत्र या अनापजत्त प्रिाणपत्र
अजनवायषता प्रिाण पत्र या अनापजत्त प्रिाण पत्र ---------------------------------- को िारी ककया िाता व ै ---- (आवेिक का
नाि) द्वारा संिाजलत िौिूिा स्नातक कायषक्रि ि ें सीटों की सख्ं या या छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता या प्रवेि क्षिता को ------ से ------
तक बढाने के जलए -------------------------------------------------- -- (कॉलेि या संस्ट्थान का नाि) ------------------------
------------------------------------------- (कॉलेि या सस्ट्ं थान का पता)। यव प्रिाणपत्र उपरोि जववरण, तथ्यों या ितों को
ध्यान ि ेंरखत े हुए िारी ककया िाता व।ै
यव प्रिाणपत्र प्रिाणपत्र िारी वोने की तारीख स ेलगातार िो िैक्षजणक सत्रों के जलए वैध व।ै
अजनवायतष ा प्रिाणपत्र या अनापजत्त प्रिाण पत्र जनम्नजलजखत जनयि और ितों पर िारी ककया िाता व:ै
1. कॉलेि भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग के तवत भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष से उजित
अनुिजत प्राप्त करने के बाि वी भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोड ष द्वारा स्ट्वीकृत छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता के
अनुसार छात्रों को प्रवेि िेगा।
2. कॉलेि छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता के अनुसार भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा जनर्िष्टष बुजनयािी ढांि,े िानव
संसाधन और कायषक्षिता के संिभष िें सभी न्द्यूनति आवश्यक िानकों को बनाए रखगे ा।
3. कॉलेि भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा बनाए गए िौिूिा जनयिों, कििाजनिेिों और नीजतयों के अनुसार
" भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग -राष्ट्रीय पात्रता-सव-प्रवेि परीक्षा सोवा-ररग्पा स्नातक" पात्र छात्रों को प्रवेि
िेगा।
4. संस्ट्थान वर सिय स्ट्वायत्त बोडष, भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग, भारत सरकार और जवश्वजवयालालय द्वारा
जनधाषररत ितों का पालन करेगा।
5. यकि आवेिक भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा जनर्िष्टष न्द्यूनति आवश्यक िानकों के अनुसार सोवा-ररग्पा
िेजडकल कॉलेि के जलए बुजनयािी ढांिे, िानव संसाधन और अन्द्य सुजवधाओं को बनान े या बनाए रखने ि ें जवफल रवता वै,
तो िेजडकल द्वारा नए प्रवेि रोक किए िाते व।ैं भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष और भारतीय जिककत्सा
पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष या भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग की अनुिजत से जवश्वजवयालालय कॉलेि ि ें पवल े
से वी प्रवेजित छात्रों की जिम्िेिारी लगे ा।
6. आयोग द्वारा जनधाषररत न्द्यूनति आवश्यक िानकों के जलए कॉलेि का पालन न करन े के कारण भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत
आकलन और रेटटंग बोड षद्वारा कॉलेि को अनुिजत िेन े से इनकार करन े या स्ट्थायी अस्ट्वीकृजत िारी करने के िािले िें, राज्य
सरकार उन छात्रों की जिम्िेिारी लगे ी िो पवले स े वी भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत आकलन और रेटटंग बोडष की अनुिजत स े
कॉलेि िें भती वो िुके व।ैं

क्षिता बढान ेके जलए आविे न ििा करन ेकी पवू -ष आवश्यकता)

3 जवश्वजवयालालय का प्रकार केंरीय या राज्य या िाजनत-सरकार या िाजनत-जनिी या जनिी

ररग्पा िेजडकल कॉलेिों की संख्या।
संबद्धता की सविजत
स्ट्थानीय िांि सजिजत की ररपोटष के आधार पर जवश्वजवयालालय, सैद्धांजतक रूप से संबद्धता की सविजत िारी करन े के जलए
सवित व ै---------------------- (कॉलेि का नाि) छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता के साथ ---------------- - प्रस्ट्ताजवत कॉलेि की (परं व
या तीस) सीटें या सीटों की संख्या या छात्र प्रवेि क्षिता या प्रवेि क्षिता ि ें---------------- से ------- तक वृजद्ध -------
पवले स ेिौिूि स्नातक कायषक्रि िें।
संबद्धता की सविजत िैक्षजणक वषष(वषों) …………… के जलए िारी की िाती व ै
संबद्धता की सविजत जनम्नजलजखत जनयिों और ितों पर िारी की िाती वःै
1. कॉलेि भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा जनर्िष्टष बुजनयािी ढांि,े िानव संसाधन और कायषक्षिता के संिभ ष
ि ें सभी न्द्यूनति आवश्यक िानकों को बनाए रखगे ा।
2. कॉलेि संबंजधत जनयिों और कििाजनििे ों ि ें भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा जनर्िष्टष केंरीय परािि ष
प्रकक्रया के िाध्यि स े "भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग -राष्ट्रीय पात्रता-सव-प्रवेि परीक्षा सोवा-ररग्पा स्नातक"
योग्य छात्रों को प्रवेि िेगा।
3. कॉलेि भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग द्वारा जनर्िष्टष पाठ्यक्रि और पाठ्यियाष के अनुसार जिक्षण और
प्रजिक्षण के जनधाषररत घंटों का संिालन सुजनजित करेगा।
4. कॉलेिों को प्रवेि प्रकक्रया िरूु वोन े स े कि स े कि तीन िवीने पवले वर साल संबद्धता की जनरंतरता प्राप्त करनी वोगी।
5. अन्द्य जवश्वजवयालालय स े सबं द्धता बिलन े या डीम्ड जस्ट्थजत के जलए आवेिन करने की जस्ट्थजत ि ें वतषिान संबद्ध
जवश्वजवयालालय स े पूवष 'अनापजत्त प्रिाणपत्र' प्राप्त ककया िाएगा।
6. वतषिान जवश्वजवयालालय स े असंबद्धता की जस्ट्थजत ि,ें िौिूिा बैि अंजति छात्र को जडग्री प्रिान वोने तक वतषिान
जवश्वजवयालालय के साथ िारी रवगें े।

प्रवेि क्षिता वाले कॉलेि)-एक अंक (अजधकति
िस अंक)
(ii) जपछले एक वषष िें प्रत्येक अजतररि बीस
रोगी जवभाग जबस्ट्तर किनों के जलए (तीस छात्र
प्रवेि क्षिता वाले कॉलेि)-एक अंक (अजधकति
िस अंक)

[नोटः यकि भारतीय जिककत्सा पद्धजत राष्ट्रीय आयोग (स्नातक सोवा-ररग्पा िवाजवध्यालय और सलं ग्न अस्ट्पतालों के जलए
आवश्यक न्द्यनू ति िानक, आकलन और रेटटंग) जवजनयि, 2023 के लविं ी और अग्रं िे ी सस्ट्ं करण के बीि कोई जवसगं जत पाई
िाती व,ै तो अग्रं िे ी सस्ट्ं करण को अजं ति िाना िाएगा।]
THE NATIONAL COMMISSION FOR INDIAN SYSTEM OF MEDICINE
NOTIFICATION
New Delhi, the 28th December, 2023
File No. 18-12/2022-BUSS (Sowa-Rigpa-UG-MES).—In exercise of the powers conferred by clauses (d),
(e), (s), (t), (u), (w), (x), (y), (z), (za), (zb) and (zc) of sub-section (2) and sub-section (1) of section 55 of the National
Commission for Indian System of Medicine Act, 2020 (14 of 2020), and in supersession of the Indian Medicine
Central Council (Requirements of Minimum Standards for Under-graduate Sowa-Rigpa Colleges and Attached
Hospitals) Regulations, 2017 and the Establishment of New Medical College, Opening of New or Higher Course of
Study or Training and Increase of Admission Capacity by a Medical College Regulations, 2019, except as respects
things done or omitted to be done before such supersession, the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine
hereby makes the following regulations, namely:-
CHAPTER-I
PRELIMINARY
1. Short title and commencement.- (1) These regulations may be called the National Commission for Indian System
of Medicine (Minimum Essential Standards, Assessment and Rating for Undergraduate Sowa-Rigpa Colleges and
Attached Teaching Hospitals) Regulations, 2023.
(2) They shall come into force on the date of their publication in the Official Gazette.
2. Definition.- (1) In these regulations, unless the context otherwise requires,-
(a) “Act” means the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine Act, 2020 (14 of 2020);
(b) “annexure” means an annexure appended to these regulations;
(c) “appendix” means an appendix appended to these regulations;
(d) “applicant” means an authority representing a society, trust, University, or any other body, but does not
include the Central Government;
(e) “assessment” of a college or institution means the act of verifying the availability of minimum essential
standards as specified in these regulations in terms of infrastructure, human resources, and functionality of an
institution and its attached teaching hospital;
(f) “attached teaching hospital” means the teaching hospital attached to the Sowa-Rigpa medical college or
institution that offers standard healthcare services to the public and teaching or training to the students of the
Sowa-Rigpa system of medicine;
(g) “educational ecosystem” means an ecosystem where, among all the stakeholders of the medical college or
institution, all the departments and other units of the college or institution function in coordination and
collaboration with each other to provide comprehensive education to students in an appropriate academic
environment;
(h)“fully established institution” means an college or institution that has completed all phase-wise
establishments under Section 29 of the Act, issued a letter of permission, received the first, second, and third
renewals of permission, and is considered fully established under Section 28 of the Act in the successive years
after the third renewal of permission;
(i) “functionality of the hospital” means an attached teaching hospital fulfilling all the minimum essential
standard requirements as specified by the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine that offers
clinical training to medical students and provides medical services including consultation, diagnosis (clinical

62 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
and investigational), treatment (medical, surgical, and procedural), preventive health care, medical advice,
counselling, nursing care, medicine dispensing, public outreach activities with proper documentation, and
maintaining a hospital management system; and shall be ready to treat or attend any type of patient at any point
in time with its manpower and infrastructure;
(j)“functionality of the college or institution” means a Sowa-Rigpa college or institution fulfilling all the
minimum essential standards as specified by the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine that
offers teaching and training to students of Sowa-Rigpa as per the course curriculum and syllabus specified by
the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine by establishing an education ecosystem;
(k) “institution under establishment” means the college or institution undergoing phase-wise establishments
(first, second, third, and final phases of establishments) under Section 29 of the Act;
(l) “letter of intent” means preliminary approval along with conditions and timelines issued by the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine to the applicant through the procedure mentioned
in these regulations to establish a new Sowa-Rigpa college or institution or to increase seats or student intake
capacity or admission capacity in existing courses or programmes or to start any new or postgraduate
programme recognised by the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine;
(m) “letter of permission” means permission granted to the applicant by the Medical Assessment and Rating
Board for Indian System of Medicine through the procedure mentioned in these regulations to establish a new
Sowa-Rigpa college or institution or to increase seats or student intake capacity or admission capacity in
existing courses or programmes or to start a postgraduate or new programme recognised by the National
Commission for Indian System of Medicine and to admit the students as per the sanctioned student intake
capacity sanctioned by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine;
(n) “minimum essential standards” means mandatory minimum requirements in terms of infrastructure, human
resources, and functionality, as well as a level of quality or standard that is thought to be acceptable as a
minimum and below the minimum, which is unacceptable;
(o) “person” means any society, trust, University, or any other body, but does not include the Central
Government;
(p) “rating” of a college or institution means rating of a fully established existing recognised college or
institution under Section 28 of the Act through a rating procedure carried out by the Medical Assessment and
Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine based on criteria or standards over and above the minimum
essential standards as laid down by the Board of Unani, Siddha and Sowa-Rigpa in these regulations;
(q) “renewal of permission” means renewed permission (i.e., first, second, and third renewal) granted by the
Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine to a new college or institution under
establishment (i.e., undergoing second, third, and fourth phase-wise establishments) through the procedures as
mentioned in these regulations during successive academic years after the issuance of a letter of permission on
fulfillment of minimum essential standards as mentioned in phase-wise establishments, for admitting students
as per the sanctioned student intake capacity for that particular academic year;
(r)“sanctioned student intake capacity” means the number of seats sanctioned or permitted by the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine to a recognised college or institution for
admission of students in a specified academic course or programme for that particular academic year;
(2) Words and expressions used in these regulations and not defined herein but defined in the Act, shall have the
respective meanings assigned to them in the Act.
CHAPTER-II
INSPECTION OR VISITATION AND ASSESSMENT OF FULLY ESTABLISHED EXISTING
SOWA-RIGPA MEDICAL COLLEGES OR INSTITUTIONS UNDER SECTION 28 OF THE ACT
3. Assessment of fully established existing colleges under section 28 of the Act.- Assessment shall be the act of
verifying the availability of the minimum essential standards of a college or institution in terms of infrastructure,
human resources, and functionality as mentioned in these regulations through the assessment procedure determined by
the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine from time to time; it shall be for the grant or
denial of permission for admission of students or to take such measures mentioned in clause (f) of sub-section (1) of
section 28 of the Act.
(1) Fulfillment of minimum essential standards to grant permission.- (a) fully-established existing Sowa-Rigpa
colleges or institutions and their attached hospitals under section 28 of the Act, shall fulfil all minimum essential

[भाग III—खण् ड 4] भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण 63
standards for infrastructure, teaching and training facilities, human resources and functionalities referred to in
these regulations 4 to 6 and Schedule- I to XIII;
(b) each college or institution shall submit a compliance report on the fulfilment of the minimum essential
standard requirements as mentioned in these regulations on or before 31st day of December of every year for
consideration of the grant of permission for taking admissions in the upcoming or next academic year;
(c) the inspection or visitation proforma as prescribed by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian
System of Medicine on the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine website for annual disclosure,
shall be filled and submitted by the colleges or institutions online or offline within the period as specified by
the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine from time to time;
(d) the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall determine the procedure for
inspection or visitation, and assessment of college or institution in accordance with standards laid down by the
Board of Unani, Siddha and Sowa- Rigpa in these regulations, and the Medical Assessment and Rating Board
for Indian System of Medicine shall carry out suo-moto inspection or visitation of existing colleges or
institutions every year in between the 1st January to 30th of June to assess the fulfilment of minimum essential
standards in terms of infrastructure, facilities, human resources, and functionality as per these regulations;
(e) inspection or visitation shall be conducted on physical or virtual or hybrid mode as decided by the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine;
(f) during inspection or visitation, the visitors shall verify the data submitted by the college or institution
through the visitation proforma online or offline as specified by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for
Indian System of Medicine and submit the visitors report with the duly filled visitors proforma, documents
provided by the college or institution, and observations made by the visitors to the Medical Assessment and
Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine online or offline as specified by the Medical Assessment and
Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine along with the videography and photography of staff (teaching
staff, non-teaching staff, and hospital staff) and infrastructure taken during the inspection or visitation and
submitted by the college or institution to the visitors;
(g) after submission by the visitors, the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine
shall verify the data and documents submitted by the college and visitors;
(h) after verification,-
(i) the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall decide to grant the
permission for admitting students for the upcoming or next academic session or not;
(ii) if it is found that the college or institution has not fulfilled or failed to maintain the minimum essential
standards as specified by the Board of Unani, Siddha and Sowa-Rigpa in these regulations, the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall deny the permission for admitting
students for the coming or upcoming or next academic session or shall take such measures, including
issuing warning, imposition of monetary penalty, reducing intake, or stoppage of admission and
recommending to the commission for withdrawal of recognition under clause (f) of sub-section (1) of
section 28 of the Act;
(iii) such decision of the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine (i.e., grant
of permission or denial of permission or measures such as penalty etc.,) shall be communicated to the
college or institution by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine on or
before 30th June of each academic year;
(i) (i) in case of denial of permission by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of
Medicine, the aggrieved college or institution may prefer an appeal to the National Commission for Indian
System of Medicine within a period of thirty days of communication of such decision by the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine (as per the sub-section (3) of section 24 of the
Act) through online or offline as decided by the Commission; Appeal is made by the aggrieved college or
institution after the stipulated period of thirty days from the date of such communication as mentioned above,
such appeal by the college or institution shall not be considered by the Commission;
(ii) upon receipt of an appeal, the Commission shall examine the appeal and the aggrieved applicant shall
be given a reasonable opportunity for hearing;
(iii) if the Commission founds that the college or institution has fulfilled all minimum essential standard
requirements as per these regulations, the Commission may direct the Medical Assessment and Rating
Board for Indian System of Medicine to consider the application;

64 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
(iv) if the college or institution has not fulfilled the minimum essential standards as per these regulations,
the commission shall deny the permission and communicate the same to the college or institution within a
period of fifteen days of receipt of the appeal;
(v) in case of disapproval by the Commission, the aggrieved college or institution may prefer an appeal to
the Ministry of Ayush, Government of India within a period of fifteen days of the communication of such
decision as per sub-section (6) of section 9 of the Act or the lapse period of fifteen days from the date of an
appeal to the Commission as mentioned in sub-clause (i) [i.e. no order has been passed by the commission
within fifteen days from the date of preferring an appeal by the college or institution to the Commission];
(vi) in case of denial of permission, the college or institution shall not be eligible to admit students for the
coming or upcoming or next academic session and shall not be entitled for rating;
(j) on receipt of any complaint or the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine or
National Commission for Indian System of Medicine is cognizant of any irregularity or malpractice or
inadequacy in the fulfilment of stipulated minimum essential standard requirements as specified in these
regulations, the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine may conduct re-
inspection or re-visitation of that particular institution and for such irregularities, the college or institution shall
be liable for actions under clause (f) of sub-section (1) of section 28 of the Act;
(k) the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall verify that the teaching
faculty present in the college is not working at any other place or institution. Teachers who are physically
absent but present only "on paper" shall not be allowed by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for
Indian System of Medicine or National Commission for Indian System of Medicine, and if the institution does
so, a monetary penalty shall be imposed on the concerned college or institution as well as the concerned
teacher under clause (f) of sub-section (1) of section 28 of the Act;
(l) as per the provision under clause (e) of sub-section (1) of section 28 of the Act, the medical Assessment and
Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall make assessment status of Sowa-Rigpa medical colleges or
institutions available on the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine website or public domain
sixty days before Sowa-Rigpa central counselling conducted by the Commission for admissions every year;
(m) the annual visitation fee shall be paid as given below by way of a Demand Draft or Online Payment
(National Electronic Funds Transfer or Real Time Gross Settlement) as specified by the Medical Assessment
and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine in favour of ‘the National Commission Fund for Indian
System of Medicine’ New Delhi along with all applicable taxes;
(i) Visitation fee: Rupees one lakh (per visitation);
(ii) Digitisation fee: Rupees thirty thousand (per visitation).
(2) Requirements of minimum essential standards to grant conditional permission.- The conditional permission of
one year for a particular academic session shall be granted only to those fully established colleges or institutions
under section 28, which are fulfilling the following requirements on the basis of inspection or visitation made by
the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine between the 1st January to 30th June
every year to admit the students for the coming or upcoming or next academic session,-
(a) the requirement of hospital staff as specified in Schedule-IV;
(b) the requirement of teachers as specified in Schedule-V;
(c) the requirement of non-teaching staff as specified in Schedule-VI;
(d) the requirement of teaching hospital as specified under sub-regulation (4) of regulations 4 and sub-
regulation (1) and (2) of regulation 6;
(e) availability of a minimum of seventy-five per cent. of required equipment as specified in Schedule-VII to
Schedule-XIII;
(f) availability of college website as specified in sub-regulation (4) of regulation 6;
(g) availability of biometric attendance system as specified in sub regulation (5) of regulation 6;
(h) availability of herbal garden as specified in the Schedule -III;
(i) availability of college council as specified in the sub-regulation (3) of regulation 6;
(j) availability of minimum total constructed area of the college and hospital as specified in sub-regulation (2)
of regulation 4.

[भाग III—खण् ड 4] भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण 65
CHAPTER-III
MINIMUM ESSENTIAL STARNDARD REQUIREMENTS FOR SOWA-RIGPA MEDICAL COLLEGE
OR INSTITUTION AND ATTACHED TEACHING HOSPITAL
4. Infrastructure and Facilities.- (1) Requirement of Land.- (a) the total built up area required for adequate
infrastructure including medical college, attached teaching hospital and other infrastructure required under these
regulations, is made available in a single piece of land, not less than one acre for hilly region and two acres for
plain region, for student intake capacity up to fifteen seats. For student intake capacity from sixteen to thirty seats,
the land shall not be less than one and half acres for hilly region and three acres for plain region and in not more
than two plots at a distance not exceeding five kilometers, and the plot, if separated by a road or canal or rivulet
but connected with bridge, shall be treated as one piece of land;
(b) the land shall be owned by the college or possessed on lease, in the name of the college or institution for a
period not less than thirty years or the maximum permissible period as per rules or regulations of the respective
State Government or Union territory Administration and the renewal of permission shall, however, be required
on expiry of lease;
(c) the requirement of the size and possession of the land is not applicable for the colleges or institutions
established prior to the date of this notification, but at the end of the current lease period, such colleges shall
either own the land or get it on lease for a period not less than thirty years or the maximum permissible period
as per rules or regulations of the respective State Government or Union territory Administration, or such
colleges shall own the land on special permission by the respective State Government or Union territory
Administration.
(2) Requirement of minimum constructed area.- (a) the college and attached teaching hospital shall have the
constructed area of six hundred square meters each for students intake capacity up to fifteen seats;
(b) the college and attached hospital, which has students intake capacity of sixteen to thirty seats shall have the
constructed area of one thousand square meters each;
(c) the college and hospital shall be constructed in separate buildings as per the details specified in Schedule-I
and Schedule-II in these regulations and the requirement of separate college and hospital buildings shall be
applicable only to the colleges established after the date of this notification;
(d) the total constructed area shall be based upon the permissible Floor Area Ratio or Floor Space Index
allowed by the authority concerned or local laws or rules;
(e) for permission of the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine, a certificate
from the concerned authorities certifying or approving the constructed buildings having the required
construction area as per Schedule-I and Schedule-II;
(f) the college shall maintain other infrastructural requirements such as canteen, outdoor and indoor games
facility, civil and electrical services, security services, workshop, adequate parking space, waste management
etc;
(g) the herbal garden shall have the minimum area as prescribed in Schedule-III of these regulations.
(3) Admission capacity.- The annual student intake capacity for an undergraduate Sowa-Rigpa course or
programme shall be in the slabs of fifteen (up to fifteen) and thirty (sixteen to thirty) students. The colleges having
student intake capacity of up to fifteen and sixteen to thirty seats shall comply the minimum essential standard
requirements for up to fifteen and sixteen to thirty seats respectively, as specified in Schedule-I to Schedule-XIII in
these regulations.
(4) Requirement of Teaching Hospital.- (a) the teaching hospital shall fulfil all the statutory requirements of the
concerned State or Union territory Administration or local authority to establish and run the hospital and shall
submit the updated certified copies of such permission or clearance to the Medical Assessment and Rating Board
for Indian System of Medicine and “No objection Certificate” issued by the concerned State Government or Union
territory Administration or concerned authority;
(b) requirement of beds.- the ratio of students with number of beds shall be 3:2 for undergraduate course, as
given in the Table-1 and the distance between two beds in general ward shall not be less than one meter;
Table-1
Minimum Essential Requirement of Beds in In-Patient Department

66 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
Student intake capacity per year Minimum number of beds in In-Patient Department with
respect to 3:2 student-bed ratio
(1) (2)
up to fifteen students ten beds
Sixteen to thirty students twenty beds
(c) space requirement.-the hospital shall accommodate Out-Patient Departments and In-Patient Departments,
hospital administration section, reception, patient’s waiting area, dressing room, clinical laboratory, hospital
pharmacy or dispensary or drug store, kitchen, service rooms, medical record-room, dpyad sbyong (external
therapy and surgery) and minor operation theatre section, emergency room, store rooms, duty rooms for
doctors, nurses and other staff required for a fully functional hospital and the specification of built up area in
the attached hospital shall be as per Schedule-I in these regulations;
(d) Out-Patient Department.- the hospital shall have minimum four clinical departments, with minimum space
as mentioned in the Schedule-I and instruments and equipment as per the Schedule-XII in these regulations,
namely,-
(i) lus nad (General Medicine);
(ii) dpyad sbyong (External Therapy and Surgery);
(iii) byis nad dang mo nad (Paediatrics and Gynaecology);
(iv) gdon nad dang dug nad (Clinical Psychology and Toxicology);
(e) In-Patient Department.- (i) the In-Patient Department of the hospital shall have separate wards for male and
female patients with minimum space as per Schedule-I and instruments and equipment as per the Schedule-XII
in these regulations;
(ii) the Out-Patient Departments shall admit the patients in male and female In-Patient Department wards
and the overall beds may be divided or allotted for the departments of lus nad (General Medicine), dpyad
sbyong (External Therapy and Surgery), byis nad dang mo nad (Paediatrics and Gynaecology) and gdon
nad dang dug nad (Clinical Psychology and Toxicology) in the ratio of 4:3:2:1 respectively;
(f) Clinical Laboratory.- (i) there shall be a clinical laboratory for Clinical Diagnosis and Investigations under
tha mal nad med dang brtag thabs (Department of Disease Prevention and Sowa-Rigpa Pathology) in the
hospital with adequate space, infrastructure and facilities as specified in Schedule-I and Schedule-XI in these
regulations for carrying out the minimum basic routine, pathological, biochemical and hematological
investigations and Sowa-Rigpa clinical diagnostic methods or tools for the patients referred from Out-Patient
and In-Patient Departments of the hospital;
(ii) the Sowa-Rigpa teaching hospital may also recommend patients to the nearest recognised modern
medicine hospital or authorized diagnostic laboratory for higher hematological, biochemical, pathological,
sonographic and radiological or imaging investigations;
(g) External Therapy and Minor Operation Theatre Section.- teaching hospital shall have external therapy and
minor operation theatre section under the Department of dpyad sbyong (External Therapy and Surgery) with
minimum space as mentioned in Schedule-I and equipment and instruments as mentioned in Schedule-X in
these regulations;
(h) Speciality Clinic.- Out-patient department(s) listed under clause (d), may establish speciality clinic(s) on the
subject(s) or disease(s) confined to the department as needed, with all adequate infrastructure and facilities.
The space for the establishment of speciality clinic is over and above the requirement of minimum total
constructed area of the teaching hospital as mentioned in these regulations;
(i) Waste Management System.- each college or institution must have a policy on waste management including
bio-medical waste and well-defined arrangement for segregation and disposal. Facilities for waste management
shall be commensurate with the Central or State or Union Territory norms as applicable.
(5) Requirements of college.- (a) office support.- Principal or Dean or Director, and each department shall have
independent computer and printer facility;
(b) space requirement.- the college shall accommodate administrative section, lecture halls or class rooms,
seminar or conference or examination or multi-purpose hall, teaching departments and attached laboratory or
museum as applicable, teaching pharmacy and quality testing laboratory, central library, canteen, and the
specification of built-up area as specified in the Schedule-II and the facilities in the laboratory or museum as
specified in the Schedules-VII, VIII, IX and Schedule-XIII of these regulations;

[भाग III—खण् ड 4] भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण 67
(c) requirement of equipment, instruments, machinery, and specimens in the college including teaching
hospital.- to ensure proper provision of teaching and training materials to the students, the college shall possess
minimum seventy five per cent. of required equipment or instrument or machinery in the teaching departments,
teaching hospital, laboratories, dissection hall, library, pharmacy, museum and other units of college and
hospital, as specified under Schedule-VII to Schedule- XIII;
(d) Clinical Skill Laboratory.- (i) the college or institution shall maintain a clinical skill laboratory for Sowa-
Rigpa diagnosis and clinical application of Sowa-Rigpa medical astrology under the Department of tha mal
nad med dang brtag thabs (Diseases Prevention and Sowa-Rigpa Pathology) with adequate seating
arrangements and basic facilities including models for demonstration and to provide hands on training or
learning experience to the students for promoting their clinical skills in the areas of Sowa-Rigpa diagnosis
including pulse, urine, tongue, physical examination, and clinical application of Sowa-Rigpa basic principles
and medical astrology, which are essential for diagnosis and assessment of prognosis;
(ii) the college or institution may provide the facilities like simulators or mannequins or virtual reality for
teaching and training in the clinical skill laboratory so as to upscale clinical skills of the students. The
clinical departments shall utilise this facility to train the students;
(e) Language Laboratory.- (i) the college shall establish a language laboratory with adequate facilities like
computer with internet facility, audio-visual aids, recording facility under the Department of lo rgyus dang lta
grub (History and Fundamental Principles of Sowa-Rigpa);
(ii) language skills include Listening, Speaking, Reading and Writing of the students shall be augmented in
the language laboratory. The Language Laboratory shall transform a passive language class into an active
speaking-based learning environment;
(iii) the Bhoti-language teacher and other teachers in this department shall spend substantial time with the
students to upgrade or upscale their Bhoti language skills in communication, phonetics and articulation of
Sowa-Rigpa medical terminologies. Text, images, audio, video, and voice recordings can be integrated for
effective training;
(f) Research facility.- (i) the college has to establish research cell, constitute Institutional Ethics Committee,
provide adequate support to innovation, incubation, research activities, publication and Intellectual Property
Rights and develop institutional policy to support research activities;
(ii) the teaching departments have to guide and support the students to carry out subject-related minor
research activities in the areas such as Sowa-Rigpa basic principles, drugs, diagnostic methods, diet,
treatment, therapeutic procedures, Sowa-Rigpa medical astrology, clinical psychology, spiritual aspect of
Sowa-Rigpa, technological innovations, teaching technologies of Sowa-Rigpa and publish research papers
under the guidance of teaching faculty;
(g) Facility for Co-curricular and Extra-curricular activities.- adequate facilities shall be provided by the
college or institution for conduction of co-curricular and extra-curricular activities such as physical education,
recreation, National Service Scheme, adventure club, science club, arts club, sports club, Language (Bhoti)
club, journal club etc;
(h) Information Technology support and Communication facilities.- (i) the college or institution shall provide
internet connectivity with broadband not less than one hundred mbps to facilitate or support online teaching or
learning including elective programme, learning management system (if any), video-conferencing, webinars,
video recording of lectures or practical demonstration, faculty development and training programme, capacity
building programme, hospital management system (if any);
(ii) there shall be adequate communication network between various sections of the college and attached
teaching hospital for providing better services, coordination, and patient care;
(iii) information technology support shall be ensured in the maintenance of college website, biometric
attendance, Closed-Circuit Television surveillance and to facilitate virtual or hybrid mode visitation or
assessment process of the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine;
(i) Medical Education Unit.- (i) medical education unit shall be established by the college or institution for
conducting faculty development and training programme, quality improvement programme, orientation
programme on teaching or training technologies, curriculum management training, continuing medical
education programme etc;
(ii) the unit shall be provided with computer, laptop, internet or Wi-Fi connectivity, multi-media projector,
audio-visual system, printer, copier, photograph, and video recording facility.

68 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]

standard requirements as specified in these regulations. The timeline to establish or accommodate such
section or units from the date of notification of these regulations shall be as per the Table-2.

5. Human Resources.- (1) Hospital staff.- The minimum staff required for the attached teaching hospital shall be as
specified in Schedule-IV of these regulations.
(2) Teaching staff.- The minimum teaching staff required for the college appointed on full-time and regular basis,
shall be as specified in Schedule-V of these regulations.
(3) Non-teaching staff.- The minimum non-teaching staff (technical and other staff) required for the college or
institution shall be as specified in Schedule-VI of these regulations.

[भाग III—खण् ड 4] भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण 69
(4) The head of the institution (Principal or Director or Dean) of each Sowa-Rigpa institution shall undergo the
orientation programme or capacity building programme on “Educational Administration” conducted by the
National Commission for Indian System of Medicine within the period specified by the Commission from time to
time. It is a mandatory requirement for holding the post of the head of the institution. Failing which, he or she shall
not be considered for the post of head of the institution by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian
System of Medicine.
(5) Deputing teaching staff.- The head of the institution shall depute the teaching staff of their institution to
perform their duties assigned by the commission or its autonomous boards and attend official meetings or training
programmes or capacity building programmes conducted by the commission or its autonomous boards based on
their appointment order. In such cases, on-duty leave shall be sanctioned for the duty days specified in the official
communication of the Commission, along with the days of travel.
6. Functionality of the College and Attached Teaching Hospital.- (1) Bed occupancy and Out-Patient Department
Attendance.- The ratio of students with number of beds shall be 3:2, In-Patient Department bed occupancy shall be
minimum thirty per cent. and Out-Patient Department attendance shall be 1:2 for undergraduate course, as given in
Table-3.

To calculate the number of beds occupied, the college shall maintain the date and time of admission and discharge
of each patient. The bed occupied by a patient at mid-night, shall be counted as one bed day occupied and if a
patient is discharged before mid-night that shall be counted as 0.5 bed day occupied. To calculate bed occupancy
following formula shall be applicable-

(2) Maintenance of record of Out-Patient Department and In-Patient Department.- The college and hospital shall
maintain the computerised central and departmental registration system for maintaining the records of patients in
Out-Patient Department and In-Patient Department; shall maintain the Out-Patient Department and In-Patient
Department records or registers, case papers or sheets of Out-Patient Department and In-Patient Department
patients, laboratory and radiological investigation registers, dpyad sbyong (External Therapy and Surgery) and
Minor operation theatre registers, medicines dispensing register, pharmacy stock registers, pharmacy indent or
supply order register, diet register for In-Patient Department patients, duty roster of hospital staff, death certificates
so as to substantiate fully functional Sowa-Rigpa hospital and shall be fulfilling the requirements as specified in
sub-regulation (4) of regulation 4 and sub-regulation (1) of regulation 6.
(3) College Council.- (a) every Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution shall have a college council comprising
of Head of Departments and the Medical Superintendent or Deputy Medical Superintendent as members and
Principal or Dean or Director as chairperson;
(b) the college council shall meet minimum four times in a year to express views on annual plan, budget,
establishments, developments, maintenance of academic standards, curriculum and training programme,
enforcement of discipline, other academic matters, co-curricular and extra-curricular activities; and
(c) the college council shall also organise inter-departmental meetings, grand rounds, statistical meetings and
clinical meetings including periodical research review in the institution regularly.
(4) College Website.- Each and every college or institution shall have its own website wherein the following
details updated in the first week of every month,-

70 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
(a) details of Principal or Dean or Director and Medical Superintendent including their name, age, photograph,
State or National registration number, qualification, date of joining, unique teacher’s code residential address
with mobile numbers and e-mail ID;
(b) details of teaching staff along with their photograph, designation, teaching department, academic
qualification, unique teacher’s code, State or National registration number, date of birth, total teaching
experience along with the name of previous institutions (if any), date of joining, permanent address, contact
number and e-mail ID;
(c) details of non-teaching staff of the college and hospital staff of the attached teaching hospital with their
position, qualification, joining date and name of the department or unit or section;
(d) details of the sanctioned student intake capacity of undergraduate programme;
(e) list of students admitted, merit-wise, category-wise in the current and previous academic session or year;
(f) any research publications by the staff or student during the last one year;
(g) details of continuing medical education programmes, conferences, seminars, workshops etc. conducted by
the college or institution;
(h) details of award and achievement received by the students or faculty or institution;
(i) details of the affiliated University and its vice-chancellor and registrar along with their contact details;
(j) result of all the university examinations of last one year;
(k) detailed status of recognition or permission (letter of permission and current permission status of the
college or institution) for conducting undergraduate course and admitting students;
(l) details of clinical material or facilities or specialities in the hospital;
(m) the college website to be linked with the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine website,
which shall be linked to the Ministry of AYUSH website;
(n) the month-wise statement of attendance of teaching, non-teaching college staff, hospital staff, students,
interns and patients in out-patient department and in-patient department; and
(o) academic calendar for the current academic session.
(5) Biometric Attendance.- There shall be biometric attendance system for teaching staff, non-teaching college
staff and hospital staff as specified by National Commission for Indian System of Medicine from time to time.
(6) Institutional Academic Committee.- (a) each college or institution shall have an institutional academic
committee as per the university guidelines, and if such guidelines are not available, the college or institutions shall
establish an institutional academic committee by comprising one higher faculty member or a faculty member from
each department of the college, the medical superintendent or deputy medical superintendent of the hospital as
members, and the head of the college or institution as the chairperson;
(b) the committee shall conduct meetings as and when necessary to plan or review the academic or clinical
activities of the college, to ensure lecture and non-lecture classes, including practical and clinical training, are
conducted as per the academic calendar, curriculum, and syllabus, and to ensure formative and summative
assessments are conducted as per the timetable or academic or examination calendar;
(c) the committee shall conduct academic audits and reports and monitor all co-curricular and extra-curricular
activities of the college.
(7) Student Support and Guidance Cell.- Each college or institution shall have a student support and guidance cell
that is intended to support and encourage students in their academic, social, emotional, and personal development.
The following services come under the purview of the student support and guidance cell,-
(a) to provide individualised counselling for the holistic development of a student by addressing academic,
scholastic, psycho-social, physical, and reproductive health issues on a need-basis;
(b) distinctive care shall be given to new batch students to become confident and competent professionals and
also to overcome academic learning-related difficulties that they face in the initial phase of their undergraduate
programme;
(c) the college shall constitute the Student Support and Guidance Cell as per the guidelines of the affiliated
university, and where such guidelines are not available, the college or institution shall constitute it as per the
following guidelines and shall make relevant guidelines for its functioning:

[भाग III—खण् ड 4] भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण 71
(i) convener (a senior faculty member);
(ii) all teaching faculty of the first professional course or programme;
(iii) each faculty member from the second and third professional courses or programmes; and
(iv) two student representatives from each batch (one male and one female);
(d) the student support and guidance cell shall deal with genuine grievances of the students in respect of the
policy defined by the college or institution; the student support and guidance cell shall investigate the reason
for such grievances and find an effective solution depending upon the merit of the grievances;
(e) the student support and guidance cell will identify opportunities for higher education and support
placements;
(f) the student support and guidance cell orient the students in preparation for various competitive examinations
and face-to-face interviews.
(8) Student Council.- (a) student council is the representative body of the entire student community of the college
or institution;
(b) student council shall be a group of ambitious, hardworking, and dedicated student leaders working together
with a faculty advisor to provide a means for expression and assistance in college affairs, conduct various
programme or institutional fest or activities, medical camps, Sowa-Rigpa promotional activities and encourage
student-faculty-community relations;
(c) the faculty advisor for student council may be a senior faculty nominated by the head of the institution;
(d) the composition of student council to be as under:-
(i) president;
(ii) secretary; and
(iii) members (one representative from each batch);
(e) the executive members of the student council shall be elected or selected or nominated by students for a
tenure of one year or as per the existing policies of the respective college or institution.
CHAPTER-IV
MINIMUM ESSENTIAL STANDARD REQUIREMENTS TO ESTABLISH A NEW SOWA-RIGPA
UNDERGRADUATE MEDICAL COLLEGE OR INSTITUTION OR
TO INCREASE THE NUMBER OF SEATS IN AN EXISTING UNDERGRADUATE PROGRAMME OR
COURSE UNDER SECTION 29 OF THE ACT
7. (1) No person shall establish a new Sowa-Rigpa medical college or increase the number of seats or student intake
capacity or admission capacity in an existing undergraduate programme or course without the prior permission of the
Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine under section 29 of the Act.
(2) Any person (society or trust or University or any other body but does not include Central Government) is
intending to establish a new Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution or to increase the number of seats, student
intake capacity or admission capacity in any existing course recognised by the National Commission for Indian
System of Medicine shall follow the criteria and procedure as mentioned in regulations 8 to 13 and shall submit a
scheme or application in such form specified in regulation 8 and Annexures-I and II, containing such particulars
accompanied by specified application fee and in such manner as specified in these regulations to the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine.
8. Application Form of Scheme.- (1) Any person (applicant) intending to establish a new Sowa-Rigpa medical
college or institution shall submit the application or scheme or proposal through online or offline in Form-1
(Annexure-I) as amended from time to time, in such manner along with required documents or particulars or
enclosures, and non-refundable application fee as mentioned in these regulations.
(2) Any Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution intending to increase the number of seats or student intake
capacity or admission capacity in any existing course recognised by the National Commission for Indian System of
Medicine shall submit the application through online or offline in Form-2 (Annexure-II) as amended from time to

72 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
time, in such manner along with required documents or particulars or enclosures and non-refundable application
fee as mentioned in these regulations.
(3) General instructions: (a) the last date for the receipt of application shall be announced by the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine or displayed on National Commission for Indian
System of Medicine website every year;
(b) incomplete applications shall not be entertained in any case;
(c) there is no provision for withdrawal of applications after last date and in such case the application fee shall
not be refunded in any case;
(d) any document of local or regional language shall be submitted in transcript of Hindi or English; and
(e) it is understood that before submission of application, the applicant should have gone through and
understood the Act, and the concerned regulations thoroughly.
9. Authority to whom the schemes or application shall be submitted.- Such application or scheme or proposal as
mentioned under regulation 8, shall be submitted through online or offline to the President, Medical Assessment and
Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine, within the period specified by the Medical Assessment and Rating
Board for Indian System of Medicine from time to time.
10. Eligibility for Making an Application.- (1) Application to establish a new Sowa-Rigpa medical college or
institution: For making an application under sub-regulation (1) of regulation 8 (Form-1), a person or applicant shall be
eligible if,-
(a) the application for establishment of new Sowa-Rigpa undergraduate medical college shall be for the student
intake capacity as specified in these regulations;
(b) at the time of submission of application or scheme or proposal, the Sowa-Rigpa hospital shall have
completed not less than one year of functionality after registration of the hospital;
(c) it is mandatory for the hospital to have the appropriate registration and shall fulfill all the statutory
requirements of the concerned State or Union territory or local authority to establish and run the hospital and
shall submit the updated certified copies of such permission or clearance to the Medical Assessment and Rating
Board for Indian System of Medicine;
(d) furnishes the documents to authenticate that, applicant’s one of the objectives is to impart Sowa-Rigpa
medical education;
(e) furnishes the documents to authenticate that the land shall be owned by the college or possessed on lease, in
the name of the college for a period not less than thirty years or the maximum permissible period as per rules or
regulations of the respective State Government or Union territory Administration and renewal shall be required
on expiry of lease; and
(i) for student intake capacity up to fifteen seats, a single piece of land not less than one acre for hilly region
and two acres for plain region;
(ii) for student intake capacity from sixteen to thirty seats, the land shall not be less than one and half acres
for hilly region and three acres for plain region and in not more than two plots at a distance not exceeding
five kilometers; and the plot, if separated by a road or canal or rivulet but connected with a bridge, shall be
treated as one piece of land;
(f) furnishes ‘No Objection Certificate’ or ‘Essentiality Certificate’ in Form-3 (Annexure-III) from the
concerned State or Union territory Administration for establishing a new Sowa-Rigpa medical college or
institution at the proposed site;
(g) furnishes ‘Consent of Affiliation’ in Form-5 (Annexure-V) from the university established under any
Central or State statute for establishing a new Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution;
(h) furnishes an undertaking that, owns and manages a hospital in Sowa-Rigpa and in a position to establish
infrastructure and manpower in phased manner (phase-wise establishments and specific requirements for new
colleges) laid down in these regulations;
(i) furnishes an undertaking that, selection or admission of students shall be made strictly through counselling
on the basis academic merit of the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine-National Eligibility-
cum-Entrance Test for Sowa-Rigpa Undergraduate programme as specified in the National Commission for
Indian System of Medicine (Minimum Standards of Undergraduate Sowa-Rigpa Education Regulations, 2022)

[भाग III—खण् ड 4] भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण 73
and maximum number of admissions shall not exceed the sanctioned student intake capacity specified by the
Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine;
(j) furnishes an undertaking that, the nomenclature of courses and requirements of teaching staff shall be
maintained as laid down in the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine (Minimum Standards of
Undergraduate Sowa-Rigpa Education Regulations, 2022);
(k) furnishes an undertaking that, has not already admitted student in any class or standard or course or training
of the proposed Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution;
(l) furnishes an undertaking that, is in a position to pay fixed security deposit valid for a period of five years in
favour of the “the National Commission Fund for Indian System of Medicine, New Delhi” and the amount to
be paid as follows:-
(i) for the establishment of new Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution up to fifteen seats (fifteen
student intake capacity)- rupees twenty-five lakhs;
(ii) for the establishment of new Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution between sixteen to thirty seats
(thirty student intake capacity)- rupees fifty lakhs;
provided that it shall not apply to the colleges governed by the Central or State Governments or Union
territory Administration if they give an undertaking to provide funds in their plan budget regularly till
requisite facilities are fully provided as per time bound programme indicated by them.
(2) Application to increase number of seats or student intake capacity or admission capacity in existing
undergraduate programme or course recognized by the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine: For
making an application under sub-regulation (2) of regulation 8 (Form-2), a Sowa-Rigpa medical college or
institution shall be eligible if,
(a) furnishes ‘No Objection Certificate’ or ‘Essentiality Certificate’ in Form-4 (Annexure-IV) from the
concerned State or Union territory Administration for permission to increase number of seats or student intake
capacity or admission capacity;
(b) furnishes ‘Consent of Affiliation’ in Form-5 (Annexure-V) from a university established under any Central
or State statute to increase the number of seats or student intake capacity or admission capacity;
(c) furnishes an undertaking that the college is able to produce documentary evidence in support of additional
financial resources, staff, space, equipment, instruments and other infrastructure as mentioned in these
regulations notified by the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine;
(d) furnishes the documents to authenticate that the college permitted by the Medical Assessment and Rating
Board for Indian System of Medicine or the erstwhile Central Council for Indian Medicine or the Central
government for running undergraduate programme or course in Sowa-Rigpa and completed at least four years
and six months in case of undergraduate programme or course after first permission:
provided that the college or institution being owned or managed by the Central Government, or the State
Government or Union territory Administration is exempted by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board
for Indian System of Medicine, from fulfilling this criteria;
(e) furnishes an undertaking that, selection or admission of students shall be made strictly through counselling
on the basis academic merit of the National Commission for Indian System of Medicine-National Eligibility-
cum-Entrance Test for Sowa-Rigpa Undergraduate Programme as specified in the National Commission for
Indian System of Medicine (Minimum Standards of Undergraduate Sowa-Rigpa Education Regulations, 2022);
(f) furnishes an undertaking that the ratio of teaching staff and students shall be maintained as mentioned in
these regulations;
(g) furnishes an undertaking that the maximum number of admissions shall not exceed the sanctioned student
intake capacity specified by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine;
(h) furnishes an undertaking that in a position to establish infrastructure and manpower in respect of student
intake capacity in such manner as specified in these regulations;
(i) furnishes an undertaking that, is in a position to pay a fixed security deposit valid for five years in favour of
the “the National Commission Fund for Indian System of Medicine, New Delhi” and the amount to be paid as
follows,-
the security deposit amount for increasing the student intake capacity from ‘up to fifteen’ slab to ‘sixteen to
thirty’ slab is rupees twelve lakhs fifty thousand; provided that it shall not apply to the colleges governed by

74 THE GAZETTE OF INDIA : EXTRAORDINARY [PART III—SEC.4]
the State Government or Union territory Administration, if they give an Undertaking to provide funds in
their plan budget regularly till requisite facilities are fully provided as per time bound programme indicated
by them.
11. Fee to be submitted along with application.- An application along with all necessary documents or enclosures to
be submitted as mentioned under regulation 8 of these regulations shall be accompanied by the following non-
refundable application fee,-
(1) to establish a new undergraduate Sowa-Rigpa medical college or institution- rupees two lakhs fifty thousand.
(2) to increase the number of seats or student intake capacity or admission capacity in existing undergraduate
programme or course- rupees one lakh twenty-five thousand.
The non-refundable application fee shall be paid by way of demand draft or online payment (National Electronic
Fund Transfer or Real Time Gross Settlement) as specified by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for
Indian System of medicine in favour of “the National Commission Fund for Indian System of Medicine” along
with applicable taxes.
12. Assessment and Permission under section 29.- (1) After receipt of the application or scheme or proposal to
establish a new medical college or institution or to increase the number of seats or student intake capacity or
admission capacity within the stipulated period as specified by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian
System of Medicine from time to time, the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall
scrutinise the application on the basis of,-
(a) eligibility criteria;
(b) application fee;
(c) No Objection Certificate or Essentiality Certificate issued by the State Government or Union territory
Administration;
(d) Consent of Affiliation issued by the University; and
(e) documents, affidavit, undertaking, as listed in Annexures I, and II as applicable, submitted by the college or
institution.
(2) The ineligible and incomplete applications without mandatory documents as specified in these regulations shall
be rejected and returned to the applicant by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of
Medicine; however, before such rejection, the applicant shall be given an opportunity by the Medical Assessment
and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine to rectify the shortcomings within the time period as mentioned
by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine.
(3) If the application is considered eligible after scrutiny, the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian
System of Medicine shall inspect or visit the college (physical or virtual or hybrid mode or as decided by the
Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine) and if the applicant college or institution is
found eligible as specified in the regulation 10, the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of
Medicine shall issue Letter of Intent.
(4) After issuance of Letter of Intent, based on the compliance report submitted by the college or institution, the
Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall again inspect or visit the college or
institution and verify the compliance or fulfillment of the minimum essential standard requirements of teaching or
training or research, the minimum essential standard requirements for infrastructure, facility, teaching faculty,
human resources, functionality and other requirements specified for first phase of establishment (as specified in the
sub-regulation (1) of regulation 13 in these regulations for new colleges) or requirements as per the student intake
capacity and other conditions of Letter of Intent; and accordingly the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for
Indian System of Medicine shall issue an order either approving (Letter of Permission) or disapproving (Denial of
Permission) the application or scheme or proposal within six months from the date of receipt of such scheme or
proposal or application;

[भाग III—खण् ड 4] भारत का रािपत्र : असाधारण 75
Provided that before disapproving such eligible application or scheme, an opportunity to rectify the defects
shall be given to the person or applicant by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of
Medicine.
(5) If the permission is denied or where after the submission of the application or scheme or proposal by the
applicant in such form with all particulars along with specified fee, no order is passed by the Medical Assessment
and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine within six months of submitting an application or proposal or
scheme, the aggrieved applicant may prefer a first appeal (through online or offline as specified by the
Commission) to the Commission within fifteen days of such denial or disapproval or after lapse of six months as
the case may be.
(6) Upon receipt of appeal, the Commission shall examine the appeal and the applicant shall be given an
opportunity for hearing through online or offline as decided by the commission.
(7) After hearing, in case, if the Commission found that the applicant is fulfilling all requirements of minimum
essential standards as specified in these regulations, the Commission may direct the Medical Assessment and
Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine to consider the application; In case, if the applicant is not fulfilling
the minimum essential standard requirements, the Commission shall disapprove or reject the application. The
Commission shall communicate such a decision to the applicant within fifteen days from the date of preferring the
appeal.
(8) Where the Commission denied or disapproved the application or proposal or scheme or no order has been
passed within fifteen days from the date of preferring first appeal under sub-regulation (5), the aggrieved applicant
or person may prefer a second appeal to the Central Government (Ministry of AYUSH) within seven days of
communication of such denial or disapproval or lapse of specified period of fifteen days.
(9) Renewal of permission of newly established college recognised under section 29.- (a) after Letter of
Permission, it is the responsibility of the college or institution to apply for the renewal of permission every year for
admitting the students for the upcoming or next academic session to the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for
Indian System of Medicine along with a compliance report with all documents before 31st December every year
and submit annual disclosure in visitation proforma as per the timeline and procedure specified by the Medical
Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine from time to time;
(b) the Letter of Permission granted by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of
Medicine to establish a new medical college or institution shall be valid for one year and it shall be renewed on
yearly basis (i.e, first renewal, second renewal and third renewal) until the college or institution is recognised
as a fully established institution under section 28 of the Act, and the details are shown in the Table-4;
(c) first renewal: the college shall submit the compliance report in respect to the fulfilment of minimum
essential standard requirements as specified in these regulations for second phase of establishment (as per the
sub-regulation (2) of regulation 13 on or before 31st day of December and annual disclosure in visitation
proforma as per the timeline and procedure specified by the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian
System of Medicine from time to time;
(d) the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall conduct inspection or
visitation, examine or scrutiny the compliance report, visitation proforma and documents submitted by the
college and observation made by the visitors in their report. On fulfilment of minimum essential standard
requirements and annual targets for second phase of establishment (as per the sub-regulation (2) of the
regulation 13), the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall issue the
renewal of permission (first renewal) on or before 30th day of June as mentioned in the regulation 15 to admit
second batch of students for the upcoming or next academic session;
(e) the same method mentioned in the above clauses (c) and (d) shall be followed for second and third renewal
of permission (for fulfilment of third and final phase of establishments respectively) to admit third and fourth
batch of students respectively as shown in the Table-4;
(f) after third renewal of permission in the succeeding years, the institution shall be treated as fully established
college or institution as per the section 28 of the Act, and shall be entitled for rating as shown in the Table-4;
(g) after third renewal, the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall visit the
college or institution suo-moto every year as per the procedure mentioned in the regulation 3 of these

regulations for fully established existing colleges for grant of permission or denial or to take such measures
mentioned in the clause (f) of sub-section (1) of section 28 of the Act and for rating;
(h) in case of non-fulfilment of minimum essential standard requirement and not attaining annual targets at any
phase of establishment of the institution under section 29, in such case, the Medical Assessment and Rating
Board for Indian System of Medicine shall deny the renewal of permission; before such denial of renewal of
permission, the Medical Assessment and Rating Board for Indian System of Medicine shall convey the
deficiencies to the applicant college and provide them an opportunity to rectify the deficiencies. In case if the
college or institution is denied the renewal of permission, the college or institution shall not admit the students
for the upcoming or next academic session;
(i) the conditional permission of one year mentioned in sub-regulation (2) of regulation 3 shall not be
applicable  for  new  colleges  i.e,  institution,  or  college  under  establishment  (undergoing  phase-wise
establishment process under section 29) and applicable only for fully established college or institution.
